<div class="se-module se-module-text"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align-left" id="SE-cb94d9e8-a5b9-4eb8-9ce9-76f3e81b086b" style=""><span class="se-fs- se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset" id="SE-1f7c7fd5-ce6c-4006-bb24-6073458d82ce" style="color:#000000;"><b>공원과 동산이 둘러쌓여있음을 의미, 풍경채라는 회사 네임을 필수로 가져가야 할 경우 이국적인 펫네임과 풍경채는 조화롭지 못함</b></span></p></div>
</td></tr><tr class="se-tr"><td class="se-cell" colspan="1" rowspan="1" style="width: 8.26%; height: 31.0px; border:none; background-color: #e2e2e2;">
<div class="se-module se-module-text"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align-center" id="SE-712a1129-2380-4105-b236-2fd4cd42bc22" style=""><span class="se-fs- se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset" id="SE-9379cadd-d838-4161-8fa9-b90d0b719ae7" style="color:#000000;"><b>74</b></span></p></div>
</td><td class="se-cell" colspan="1" rowspan="1" style="width: 44.06%; height: 31.0px; border:none; background-color: #e2e2e2;">
<div class="se-module se-module-text"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align-center" id="SE-5954fca0-2d46-40d7-9baf-7bd7f7d8eb7c" style=""><span class="se-fs- se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset" id="SE-b29881a1-ff21-4f77-a6a8-a59732157af7" style="color:#000000;"><b>검단 풍경채 (더) 클래식</b></span></p></div>
</td><td class="se-cell" colspan="1" rowspan="1" style="width: 47.67%; height: 31.0px; border:none; background-color: #e2e2e2;">
<div class="se-module se-module-text"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align-left" id="SE-263f4cdb-637d-4f0a-b8bc-45eb490915ae" style=""><span class="se-fs- se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset" id="SE-0788d0ea-02d3-45a4-ad9a-7f1e2eca7e78" style="color:#000000;"><b>풍경채 자체가 자연친화적인 의미라 별도의 단어는 생략, 세월이 흘러도 격조와 품격을 유지한다는 느낌, 클래식한 아파트를 의미</b></span></p></div>
</td></tr><tr class="se-tr"><td class="se-cell" colspan="1" rowspan="1" style="width: 8.26%; height: 31.0px; border:none; ">
<div class="se-module se-module-text"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align-center" id="SE-188a22af-b6f2-42fe-8296-885fc8d4968e" style=""><span class="se-fs- se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset" id="SE-a5cee6df-35a9-41e4-9e4b-5ac44fff8677" style="color:#000000;"><b>75</b></span></p></div>
</td><td class="se-cell" colspan="1" rowspan="1" style="width: 44.06%; height: 31.0px; border:none; ">
<div class="se-module se-module-text"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align-center" id="SE-80f90e64-1557-4e29-8d6a-2fc70bfdc2af" style=""><span class="se-fs- se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset" id="SE-642c2465-fcf6-43d9-8925-62ed6b2caac8" style="color:#000000;"><b>제일풍경채 더 그랜드</b></span></p></div>
</td><td class="se-cell" colspan="1" rowspan="1" style="width: 47.67%; height: 31.0px; border:none; ">
<div class="se-module se-module-text"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align-left" id="SE-0f34635a-fbf2-4ba7-9883-3fa144552812" style=""><span class="se-fs- se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset" id="SE-fdc9ac27-1a78-47d5-8e60-06949767b3e1" style="color:#000000;"><b>검단에서 세대 수가 가장 많다는 점을 뜻함</b></span></p></div>
</td></tr><tr class="se-tr"><td class="se-cell" colspan="1" rowspan="1" style="width: 8.26%; height: 31.0px; border:none; background-color: #e2e2e2;">
<div class="se-module se-module-text"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align-center" id="SE-229319a2-8278-4adc-ace4-c274e7036336" style=""><span class="se-fs- se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset" id="SE-6f86ce27-5737-40f8-9660-50a3c3f2a8b4" style="color:#000000;"><b>76</b></span></p></div>
</td><td class="se-cell" colspan="1" rowspan="1" style="width: 44.06%; height: 31.0px; border:none; background-color: #e2e2e2;">
<div class="se-module se-module-text"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align-center" id="SE-d1bff7c7-4bba-4862-8d4c-a0f708f1d203" style=""><span class="se-fs- se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset" id="SE-f77ef356-eb8c-4285-ac85-4a563845864f" style="color:#000000;"><b>풍경채 더 MQV(엠큐브이)</b></span></p></div>
</td><td class="se-cell" colspan="1" rowspan="1" style="width: 47.67%; height: 31.0px; border:none; background-color: #e2e2e2;">
<div class="se-module se-module-text"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align-left" id="SE-b72e551a-e1d2-4ea8-bb82-2bcd56a9e39c" style=""><span class="se-fs- se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset" id="SE-3c12be8c-f582-496f-895c-b47810ab5351" style="color:#000000;"><b>더 나은 삶의 질을 뜻하는 프랑스어들을 합성하여 표현, meilleure(더 나은, 더 좋은 등) qualite(특성, 장점, 품질 등) de vie(생명, 목숨 등)</b></span></p></div>
</td></tr><tr class="se-tr"><td class="se-cell" colspan="1" rowspan="1" style="width: 8.26%; height: 31.0px; border:none; ">
<div class="se-module se-module-text"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align-center" id="SE-ac324331-b846-44cf-8dd0-77c895a8db36" style=""><span class="se-fs- se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset" id="SE-54810d29-5a76-4437-8d5b-6f2bf8859384" style="color:#000000;"><b>77</b></span></p></div>
</td><td class="se-cell" colspan="1" rowspan="1" style="width: 44.06%; height: 31.0px; border:none; ">
<div class="se-module se-module-text"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align-center" id="SE-f4fc7be3-4cc1-4b4f-82a5-4f96b5bd9f1d" style=""><span class="se-fs- se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset" id="SE-63029fac-6fc3-49e1-816b-9c6690c4bdda" style="color:#000000;"><b>풍경채 커넥션(connection)</b></span></p></div>
</td><td class="se-cell" colspan="1" rowspan="1" style="width: 47.67%; height: 31.0px; border:none; ">
<div class="se-module se-module-text"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align-left" id="SE-7f234c71-8dfb-4b89-bcc9-81671f0df9ae" style=""><span class="se-fs- se-ff-nanummaruburi se-style-unset" id="SE-a338133e-cc73-4f92-a2dc-e8e397babf10" style="color:#000000;"><b>5차까지 있는 풍경채를 이어주고, 1차부터 3차까지 신도시를 이어준다는 것을 의미</b></span></p></div>
</td></tr></tbody>

            '<span class="inner">입예협 투표소</span>'
        </strong><span class="text">게시판 글</span></h2><div class="RelatedArticlesTabContainer" data-v-62534562="" has-no-display-tab-title="true"><div class="RelatedArticlesTabContainer__tab" data-v-62534562=""><div class="tab_area" data-v-62534562=""><!-- --><div class="tool_area" data-v-62534562=""><div class="SubscribeButton" data-v-62534562=""><em class="subscribe_text">이 게시판 새글 구독하기</em><div class="ToggleSwitch ToggleSwitch--skinGray"><input class="switch_input blind" id="4" type="checkbox"/><label class="switch_slider" for="4"><span class="blind">등록</span></label></div></div><div class="ToggleSwitchTooltip" data-v-62534562=""><div class="tooltip" style="display: none;">

            </span><!-- --></div><div class="member_area"><a class="member" href="#" id="Related52250" role="button">
                102동 코리동동
